Strategic Interpretation

After a contested opening, Saklian Watch Rebels’ Martial Coast approach created the midgame break because they gained 6 regions while Yunavaun Hollow Rebels lost 4, which shifted the board from parity into a clear territorial lead. Taking the treasury lead at the same time mattered because it let that break compound rather than fade, so the later 16-region margin reflected sustained separation instead of a single swing. The early gains by other factions did not convert because the midphase reversal removed their ability to hold ground on a thirty-seven-region ring.
The closest challenger was Aruangos Tribe (Adaptive Forest) at 138 treasury and 4 regions.

Victor's History

The Saklian Watch Rebels prevailed because their Martial Coast approach produced the decisive middle-phase break, and they never surrendered the initiative afterward. They opened with 3 claims, reached 12 regions by the end of the opening phase, and then built steadily to 20 regions and 198 treasury by turn 100, while also taking the treasury lead in the midgame. The runner-up Aruangos Tribe showed some reach, peaking at 8 regions before slipping back to 4, but the contest was ultimately settled by Saklian steadiness and force of execution. On a thirty-seven-region ring, that kind of coherent advance was enough to make the result plain.
